   sarvagatatvāt- sarvagato hi śabdo bhinnadeśairdhvanibhiḥ svesve deśe	sarva-gata-tvAt sarva-gataH hi SabdaH Binna-deSEH-DvaniBiH svesve deSe

   nanu prāpyakāri śrotraṃ, na ca dhvanyutpattideśaḥ śrotreṇa prāpyata iti	nanu prApya-kAri SrotraM, na ca Dvani-utpatti-deSaH SrotreNa prApyate iti
   kathaṃ tasya śrotreṇa grahaṇam, tadagrahe ca kathaṃ tadviśiṣṭaśabdagrahaḥ	kaTam tasya SrotreNa grahaNam, tad-agrahe ca kaTam tad-viSizwa-Sabda-grahaH
